\mbox{\Hypertarget{libmmg3d__private_8h_a5546a5714d3790ef3ffd5e183833a393}\label{libmmg3d__private_8h_a5546a5714d3790ef3ffd5e183833a393}} 
\index{libmmg3d\_private.h@{libmmg3d\_private.h}!MMG3D\_analys@{MMG3D\_analys}}
\index{MMG3D\_analys@{MMG3D\_analys}!libmmg3d\_private.h@{libmmg3d\_private.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_analys()}{MMG3D\_analys()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+analys (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to mesh \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if successful, 0 if fail
\end{DoxyReturn}
preprocessing stage\+: mesh analysis.

At the end of this function\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item triangles have been deleted and stored in xtetra;
\item Boundary point have been analyzed and associated to xpoints (if needed). If computed tangent is stored in ppt-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}n and normals in pxp-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}n1 and pxp-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}n2. Following list summerizes computed (and not computed) data depending on point type\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Corner point (MG\+\_\+\+CRN)\+: no computation (and no xpoint);
\item Required points have different treatment depending if they are along a \textquotesingle{}regular\textquotesingle{} surf point, along an internal or external non-\/manifold edge, along a non connex mesh part(so they may have a xpoint, a tangent and a normal or not) but their normal is not used during remeshing. See comments in \mbox{\hyperlink{analys__3d_8c_ae07072c180158d36c144fb6c3042bf7d}{MMG3\+D\+\_\+nmgeom}}
\item Reference point (MG\+\_\+\+REF)\+: xpoint, tangent, 1 normal;
\item Ridge point (MG\+\_\+\+GEO)\+: xp, tangent,2 normals;
\item Non-\/manifold point (MG\+\_\+\+NOM)\+: xp, tangent, no normal if internal, 1 normal if external
\item Open boundary points (MG\+\_\+\+OPNBDY) are treated as nm points. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyEnumerate}--- stage 1\+: data structures for surface

--- stage 2\+: surface analysis

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_chkmanicoll()}{MMG3D\_chkmanicoll()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+chkmanicoll (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{k,  }\item[{int}]{iface,  }\item[{int}]{iedg,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ndepmin,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ndepplus,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{refmin,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{refplus,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{isminp,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{isplp }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em k} & index of element in which we collapse. \\
\hline
{\em iface} & face through wich we perform the collapse \\
\hline
{\em iedg} & edge to collapse \\
\hline
{\em ndepmin} & index of an elt with ref refmin and outside the shell of edge. \\
\hline
{\em ndepplus} & ndex of an elt with ref refplus and outside the shell of edge. \\
\hline
{\em refmin} & reference of one of the two subdomains in presence \\
\hline
{\em refplus} & reference of the other subdomain in presence \\
\hline
{\em isminp} & 1 if we have found a tetra with ref refmin \\
\hline
{\em isplp} & 1 if we have found a tetra with ref refplus \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if we create a non manifold situation, 1 otherwise
\end{DoxyReturn}
Check whether collapse of point np to nq does not create a non manifold situation at nq ndepmin, ndepplus = tetra of ref minus, plus in ball of np, not in shell of (np,nq). First step \+: pile up tetras of future ball of nq, crossing through the shell of (np,nq), as long as they have same ref as ndepmin list\mbox{[}l\mbox{]} \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= 0 if element of ball of np, \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}= 0, if element of ball of nq

Second step \+: same process, starting with a tetra of different reference, in the ball of np

\index{libmmg3d\_private.h@{libmmg3d\_private.h}!MMG3D\_curveEndingPts@{MMG3D\_curveEndingPts}}
\index{MMG3D\_curveEndingPts@{MMG3D\_curveEndingPts}!libmmg3d\_private.h@{libmmg3d\_private.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_curveEndingPts()}{MMG3D\_curveEndingPts()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+curve\+Ending\+Pts (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{lists,  }\item[{int}]{ilists,  }\item[{const uint16\+\_\+t}]{edg\+Tag,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ip0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ip1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ip2 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em lists} & pointer to the surfacic ball of the point. \\
\hline
{\em ilists} & size of the surfacic ball. \\
\hline
{\em edg\+Tag} & Type of edge on which we move (\mbox{\hyperlink{mmgcommon__private_8h_aed4613c0f3a1afbcea3325f68c87989d}{MG\+\_\+\+REF}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgcommon__private_8h_ad4f5aeeaf0e3b7260e75d2d90df0de57}{MG\+\_\+\+NOM}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgcommon__private_8h_a0776e940d2dc5be4b516dbd5ff3d30dd}{MG\+\_\+\+GEO}}). \\
\hline
{\em ip0} & point that we want to move along curve. \\
\hline
{\em ip1} & first ending point of curve (in current surfacic ball). \\
\hline
{\em ip2} & second ending point of curve (in current surfacic ball).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if fail (one of curve extremity is not found), 1 if success.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Search the two ending points of curve passing through {\itshape ip0} in the surfacic ball of {\itshape ip0}.

Travel surfacic ball and recover the two ending points of curve (that will be stored in {\itshape ip1} and {\itshape ip2})\+: ball is travelled from beginning in one direction until meeting the curve edge, then, starting from the end, in the other direction until meeting the second curve edge. a. Travel surface edges in one sense to get the first featured edge. Triangles of the surface are successively processed and the tag of the edge between current tria and previous one is tested (so each edge is checked only once). Ball processing stops at first featured edge crossed.

b. Now travel surface edges in the reverse sense so as to get the second curve. Again, we test the tag of the edge at interface of current triangle and previous one and we stop ball pocessing when the second featured edge has been found. This edge is necessarly different from the one previously found.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{movpt__3d_8c_source_l00944}{944}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{movpt__3d_8c_source}{movpt\+\_\+3d.\+c}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_defsiz\_ani()}{MMG3D\_defsiz\_ani()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+defsiz\+\_\+ani (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em met} & pointer to the metric stucture. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if fail, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Define size at points by intersecting the surfacic metric and the physical metric.


\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item On singular (CRN, REQ, NOM) points, the metric on P is made isotropic.
\item On non-\/singular ridge points, the metric is forced to be aligned with the ridge directions and surface normals.
\item On regular boundary points, the metric can be anisotropic on the tangent plane, but it is forced to be aligned to the normal direction. 
\end{DoxyEnumerate}Step 1\+: Set metric at points belonging to a required edge\+: compute the metric as the mean of the length of the required eges passing through the point

Define isotropic size map at all boundary vertices of the mesh, associated with geometric approx, and prescribe hmax at the internal vertices Field h of Point is used, to store the prescribed size (not inverse, squared,...) 1) Size at internal points

Step 1\+: Set metric at points belonging to a required edge\+: compute the metric as the mean of the length of the required eges passing through the point

Step 2\+: size at non required internal points

First step\+: search for local parameters

Second step\+: set the metric

Set size at points that cannot be reached from the tetra

First step\+: search for local parameters

Second step\+: set the metric

Set size at points that cannot be reached from the tetra

Step 3\+: size at regular surface points

First step\+: search for local parameters

Second step\+: set the metric

3) Travel all boundary faces to update size prescription for points on ridges/edges

First step\+: search for local parameters

Second step\+: set metric

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void MMG3\+D\+\_\+find\+\_\+bdyface\+\_\+from\+\_\+edge (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_aa048f146b39894e279e53fd0a209f320}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Tetra}}}]{pt,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{ied,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{i,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{j,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{i1,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{i2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ip1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ip2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a8a626fbb189129e6f22bde1246f7bb25}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Point}} $\ast$}]{p0,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a8a626fbb189129e6f22bde1246f7bb25}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Point}} $\ast$}]{p1 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to mesh \\
\hline
{\em pt} & pointer to tetra on which we work \\
\hline
{\em ied} & index in tetra {\itshape pt} of edge on which we work \\
\hline
{\em i} & index of a face of {\itshape pt} that contains {\itshape ied}. If possible we choose a boundary face with suitable orientation (to fill) \\
\hline
{\em j} & local index of edge {\itshape ied} in face {\itshape i} (to fill) \\
\hline
{\em i1} & local index in tetra {\itshape pt} of first extremity of edge {\itshape ied} (to fill) \\
\hline
{\em i2} & local index in tetra {\itshape pt} of second extremity of edge {\itshape ied} (to fill) \\
\hline

\hline
{\em ip2} & global index in tetra {\itshape pt} of second extremity of edge {\itshape ied} (to fill) \\
\hline

\hline
{\em p1} & pointer to second extremity of edge {\itshape ied} (to fill)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Search a face from wich we car reach edge {\itshape ied}. If a boundary face with good orientation exists it is choosed prior to another face, otherwise, if possible, we choose a boundary face. Fill data needed to work on edge. An edge can be at the interface of a boundary face with good orientation and of another one with bad orientation\+: ensure to treat the edge from the suitable face

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Free\_all\_var()}{MMG3D\_Free\_all\_var()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Free\+\_\+all\+\_\+var (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{va\+\_\+list}]{argptr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em argptr} & list of the mmg structures that must be deallocated. Each structure must follow one of the MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG$\ast$ preprocessor variable that allow to identify it.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
{\itshape argptr} contains at least a pointer to a {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh} structure (that will contain the mesh and identified by the MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh keyword)

To call the {\itshape MMG3\+D\+\_\+mmg3dlib} function, you must also provide a pointer to a {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol} structure (that will contain the ouput metric (and the input one, if provided) and identified by the MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Met keyword).

To call the {\itshape MMG3\+D\+\_\+mmg3dls} function, you must also provide a pointer toward a {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol} structure (that will contain the level-\/set function and identified by the MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Ls keyword).

To call the {\itshape MMG3\+D\+\_\+mmg3dmov} library, you must also provide a pointer to a {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol} structure storing the displacement (and identified by the MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Disp keyword).

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if fail, 1 if success
\end{DoxyReturn}
Internal function for deallocations before return (taking a va\+\_\+list as argument).

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
we pass the structures by reference in order to have argument compatibility between the library call from a Fortran code and a C code. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

\index{libmmg3d\_private.h@{libmmg3d\_private.h}!MMG3D\_gradsiz\_ani@{MMG3D\_gradsiz\_ani}}
\index{MMG3D\_gradsiz\_ani@{MMG3D\_gradsiz\_ani}!libmmg3d\_private.h@{libmmg3d\_private.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_gradsiz\_ani()}{MMG3D\_gradsiz\_ani()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+gradsiz\+\_\+ani (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em met} & pointer to the metric structure. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1
\end{DoxyReturn}
Enforces mesh gradation by truncating metric field.


\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item On singular (CRN, REQ, NOM) points, the metric on P is isotropic (as in MMG5\+\_\+defmetsin) and should remain isotropic.
\item On non-\/singular ridge points, the metric on P should remain aligned with the ridge directions (thus it is not possible to apply metric intersection, sizes are truncated instead).
\item On regular boundary points, the metric can be anisotropic on the tangent plane, but it should remain aligned to the normal direction (thus, intersection is used only in the tangent plane and sizes are truncated in the normal direction).
\item On interior volume points, 3D metric intersection can be used. 
\end{DoxyEnumerate}Mark the edges belonging to a required entity

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Init\_mesh\_var()}{MMG3D\_Init\_mesh\_var()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh\+\_\+var (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{va\+\_\+list}]{argptr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em argptr} & list of the mmg structures that must be initialized. Each structure must follow one of the MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG$\ast$ preprocessor variable that allow to identify it.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
{\itshape argptr} contains at least a pointer to a {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh} structure (that will contain the mesh and identified by the MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh keyword)

To call the {\itshape MMG3\+D\+\_\+mmg3dlib} function, you must also provide a pointer to a {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol} structure (that will contain the ouput metric (and the input one, if provided) and identified by the MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Met keyword).

To call the {\itshape MMG3\+D\+\_\+mmg3dls} function, you must also provide a pointer toward a {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol} structure (that will contain the level-\/set function and identified by the MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Ls keyword).

To call the {\itshape MMG3\+D\+\_\+mmg3dmov} library, you must also provide a pointer to a {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol} structure storing the displacement (and identified by the MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Disp keyword).

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if success, 0 if fail
\end{DoxyReturn}
Internal function for structure allocations (taking a va\+\_\+list argument). 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{variadic__3d_8c_source_l00177}{177}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{variadic__3d_8c_source}{variadic\+\_\+3d.\+c}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_memOption\_memSet()}{MMG3D\_memOption\_memSet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+mem\+Option\+\_\+mem\+Set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if fail, 1 otherwise
\end{DoxyReturn}
Set the mem\+Max value to its \char`\"{}true\char`\"{} value (50\% of the RAM or memory asked by user) and perform memory repartition for the -\/m option. If -\/m is not given, mem\+Max is the detected RAM. If -\/m is provided, check the user option and set mem\+Max to the available RAM if the user ask for too much memory. Last, perform the memory repartition between the mmg arrays with respect to the mem\+Max value.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Here, mesh-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}npmax/nemax/ntmax must be setted. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

\end{DoxyReturn}
Check volumes of the tetra in the ball of point with new position of point. Update coordinates, normals, tangents and qualities if point displacement is accepted. Check wether all volumes remain positive with new position of the point

Update coordinates, normals, for new point

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_nmgeom()}{MMG3D\_nmgeom()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+nmgeom (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if fail, 1 otherwise
\end{DoxyReturn}
Define continuous geometric support at non manifold vertices, using volume information.

Following list summerizes computed data depending on point type\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Non-\/manifold external point along connex mesh part (MG\+\_\+\+NOM)\+: xp, tangent, normal n1, nnor=0
\item Non-\/manifold external point along edge or point connected mesh part (MG\+\_\+\+NOM)\+: no xp,no tangent,no normal,nnor=0
\item Non-\/manifold not required internal point (MG\+\_\+\+NOM+\+MG\+\_\+\+REQ)\+: xp, tangent, no normal, nnor=1.
\item Non-\/manifold required internal point (MG\+\_\+\+NOM+\+MG\+\_\+\+REQ)\+: no xp, no tangent, no normal, nnor=1.
\item Non-\/manifold open-\/boundary (MG\+\_\+\+OPNBDY) edges are treated like others\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item if we are along a \char`\"{}truly\char`\"{} open boundary, it is an internal nm edge so we don\textquotesingle{}t have any normal;
\item if the edge is marked as open while being only non-\/manifold, we may compute a normal (along an external boundary) or not (along an internal one).
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item We don\textquotesingle{}t compute anything along corner points. 
\end{DoxyItemize}

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{analys__3d_8c_source_l01198}{1198}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{analys__3d_8c_source}{analys\+\_\+3d.\+c}}.

\index{libmmg3d\_private.h@{libmmg3d\_private.h}!MMG3D\_rotate\_surfacicBall@{MMG3D\_rotate\_surfacicBall}}
\index{MMG3D\_rotate\_surfacicBall@{MMG3D\_rotate\_surfacicBall}!libmmg3d\_private.h@{libmmg3d\_private.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_rotate\_surfacicBall()}{MMG3D\_rotate\_surfacicBall()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+rotate\+\_\+surfacic\+Ball (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{lists,  }\item[{int}]{ilists,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ip0,  }\item[{double}]{r\mbox{[}3\mbox{]}\mbox{[}3\mbox{]},  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{lispoi }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em lists} & pointer to the surfacic ball of the point. \\
\hline
{\em ilists} & size of the surfacic ball. \\
\hline
{\em ip0} & global index of the point that we move \\
\hline
{\em r} & rotation matrix that sends the normal at {\itshape ip0} to z-\/axis \\
\hline
{\em lispoi} & rotated surfacic ball (lispoi\mbox{[}k\mbox{]} is the common edge between faces lists\mbox{[}k-\/1\mbox{]} and lists\mbox{[}k\mbox{]})\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if success, 0 if the projection along the tangent plane are invalid.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Rotation of the oriented surfacic ball of {\itshape ip0}. At this point, lispoi contains the oriented surface ball of point p0, that has been rotated through r, with the convention that triangle l has edges lispoi\mbox{[}l\mbox{]}; lispoi\mbox{[}l+1\mbox{]}

Compute vertices and edges permutation for the split of 2 edge along the same face. The configuration flag is computed such as the i$^\wedge$th bit of flag is 1 if the i$^\wedge$th edge is splitted).

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_swap23()}{MMG3D\_swap23()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+swap23 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{k,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{met\+Rid\+Typ,  }\item[{int}]{ifac,  }\item[{int}]{conf0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{adj,  }\item[{int}]{conf1 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em met} & pointer to the sol structure. \\
\hline
{\em k} & index of the tetrahedron with multiple boundary faces (to be swapped). \\
\hline
{\em met\+Rid\+Typ} & metric storage (classic or special) \\
\hline
{\em ifac} & face of the tetra {\itshape k} that give the best results for the swap23 \\
\hline
{\em conf0} & detected configuration for the swap23 of the tetra {\itshape k} \\
\hline
{\em adj} & neighbour of the tetra k through the face {\itshape ifac} (4$\ast$k1+ifac1) \\
\hline
{\em conf1} & detected configuration for the swap23 of the tetra {\itshape adj/4} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
-\/1 if lack of memory, 0 if fail to swap, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Search an adjacent to the tetra {\itshape k} and perform swap 2-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}3 (the common face of the 2 tetra is destroyed and replaced by a common edge used by the three new elts).

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
used in anatet4 to remove the tetra with multiple boundary faces. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
Neighbouring element with which we will try to swap

Swap

Quality Update

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG5\+\_\+bdry\+Update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if successful, 0 if not.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Update tag and refs of tetra edges. If tetra is required, set the faces/edges to required.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
While remeshing\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item A tetra with a boundary face has a xtetra\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item a boundary edge has consistent tags as soon as it has a non 0 tag; \#warning check this case
\item some boundary edges may have a 0 tag
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyRemark}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item a tetra with a boundary edge but no bdy faces may or may not have a xtetra and boundary edges may have or may not have tags so we can\textquotesingle{}t guess nothing with such xtetra. 
\end{DoxyItemize}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG5\+\_\+boulenm\+Int (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{start,  }\item[{int}]{ip,  }\item[{double}]{t\mbox{[}3\mbox{]} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
{\em t} & computed tangent vector. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 when more than two NOM points are attached to ip, 1 if sucess.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Travel the ball of the internal non manifold point ip in tetra start and calculate the tangent vector to the underlying curve.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
we are not able to compute tangent along non-\/manifold points for edge-\/connected meshes. In this case the point doesn\textquotesingle{}t have xpoint nor tangent or normal. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG5\_boulesurfvolp()}{MMG5\_boulesurfvolp()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG5\+\_\+boulesurfvolp (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{start,  }\item[{int}]{ip,  }\item[{int}]{iface,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{listv,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{ilistv,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{lists,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{ilists,  }\item[{int}]{isnm }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em start} & index of the starting tetra. \\
\hline
{\em ip} & index in {\itshape start} of the looked point. \\
\hline
{\em iface} & index in {\itshape start} of the starting face. \\
\hline
{\em listv} & pointer to the computed volumic ball. \\
\hline
{\em ilistv} & pointer to the computed volumic ball size. \\
\hline
{\em lists} & pointer to the computed surfacic ball. \\
\hline
{\em ilists} & pointer to the computed surfacic ball size. \\
\hline
{\em isnm} & 1 if {\itshape ip} is non-\/manifold, 0 otherwise. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
-\/1 if fail, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Compute the volumic ball of a SURFACE point {\itshape p}, as well as its surfacic ball, starting from tetra {\itshape start}, with point {\itshape ip}, and face {\itshape if} in tetra volumic ball\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\itshape listv}\mbox{[}k\mbox{]} = 4$\ast$ tet index + index of point surfacic ball.
\item {\itshape lists}\mbox{[}k\mbox{]} = 4$\ast$ tet index + index of boundary face.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Don\textquotesingle{}t work for a non-\/manifold point if {\itshape start} has an adjacent through {\itshape iface} (for example \+: a non-\/manifold subdomain). Thus, if {\itshape ip} is non-\/manifold, must be called only if {\itshape start} has no adjacent through iface. 
\end{DoxyWarning}


Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{boulep__3d_8c_source_l00610}{610}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{boulep__3d_8c_source}{boulep\+\_\+3d.\+c}}.

\index{libmmg3d\_private.h@{libmmg3d\_private.h}!MMG5\_boulesurfvolpNom@{MMG5\_boulesurfvolpNom}}
\index{MMG5\_boulesurfvolpNom@{MMG5\_boulesurfvolpNom}!libmmg3d\_private.h@{libmmg3d\_private.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG5\_boulesurfvolpNom()}{MMG5\_boulesurfvolpNom()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG5\+\_\+boulesurfvolp\+Nom (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{start,  }\item[{int}]{ip,  }\item[{int}]{iface,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{listv,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{ilistv,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{lists,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{ilists,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{refmin,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{refplus,  }\item[{int}]{isnm }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em start} & index of the starting tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em ip} & index in {\itshape start} of the desired vertex. \\
\hline
{\em iface} & index in {\itshape start} of the starting face. \\
\hline
{\em listv} & pointer to the computed volumic ball. \\
\hline
{\em ilistv} & pointer to the computed volumic ball size. \\
\hline
{\em lists} & pointer to the computed surfacic ball. \\
\hline
{\em ilists} & pointer to the computed surfacic ball size. \\
\hline
{\em refmin} & return the reference of one of the two subdomains in presence \\
\hline
{\em refplus} & return the reference of the other subdomain in presence \\
\hline
{\em isnm} & is the vertex non-\/manifold? \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if succesful, a negative value if the ball cannot be computed\+: -\/1 if a surface ball had too many elements, -\/2 if there are more than two references around, -\/3 if an edge cannot be found, and -\/4 if a volume ball had too many elements. Among these, -\/1, -\/3 and -\/4 can be taken as a sign that further remeshing is not possible, while -\/2 just mean the job could not be done.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Compute the volumic ball of a SURFACE point {\itshape p}, as well as its surfacic ball, starting from tetra {\itshape start}, with point {\itshape ip}, and face {\itshape if} in the volumic ball. {\itshape listv}\mbox{[}k\mbox{]} = 4$\ast$number of tet + index of point surfacic ball. {\itshape lists}\mbox{[}k\mbox{]} = 4$\ast$number of tet + index of face.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Doesn\textquotesingle{}t work for a non-\/manifold point if {\itshape start} has an adjacent through {\itshape iface} (for example\+: a non-\/manifold subdomain). Thus, if {\itshape ip} is non-\/manifold, must be called only if {\itshape start} has no adjacent through iface. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG5\+\_\+bouletrid (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{start,  }\item[{int}]{iface,  }\item[{int}]{ip,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{il1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{l1,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{il2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{l2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ip0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ip1 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\end{DoxyReturn}
Computation of the two surface balls of a ridge point\+: the list {\itshape l1} is associated to the normal of face {\itshape iface}. {\itshape ip0} and {\itshape ip1} are the indices of the 2 ending point of the ridge. Both lists are returned enumerated in direct order.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG5\+\_\+boulevolp (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{start,  }\item[{int}]{ip,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{list }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Given a vertex and a tetrahedron, find all tetrahedra in the ball of this vertex. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em start} & index of the starting tetrahedra. \\
\hline
{\em ip} & local index of the point in the tetrahedra {\itshape start}. \\
\hline
{\em list} & pointer to the list of the tetra in the volumic ball of {\itshape ip}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if fail and the number of the tetra in the ball otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Fill the volumic ball (i.\+e. filled with tetrahedra) of point {\itshape ip} in tetra {\itshape start}. Results are stored in the form $4*kel + jel$, kel = number of tetrahedra, jel = local index of p within kel.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG5\_chkBdryTria()}{MMG5\_chkBdryTria()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG5\+\_\+chk\+Bdry\+Tria (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if success, 0 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Remove double triangles from tria array.
\item Remove triangles that do not belong to a boundary (non opnbdy mode) from tria array.
\item Check the matching between actual and given number of faces in the mesh\+: Count the number of faces in mesh and compare this number to the number of given triangles.
\item If the founded number exceed the given one, add the missing boundary triangles (call to MMG5\+\_\+bdry\+Tria). Do nothing otherwise.
\item Fill the adjacency relationship between prisms and tetra (fill adjapr with a negative value to mark this special faces).
\item Set to required the triangles at interface betwen prisms and tet. 
\end{DoxyItemize}Step 1\+: scan the mesh and count the boundaries

Step 2\+: detect the extra boundaries (that will be ignored) provided by the user

Step 3\+: add the missing boundary triangles or, if the mesh contains prisms, set to required the triangles at interface betwen prisms and tet

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
{\em refmin} & reference of one of the two subdomains in presence \\
\hline

\hline

\hline
{\em isnmint} & 1 if ip is an internal non manifold point;\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
ilistv if success, 0 if the point cannot be collapsed, -\/1 if fail.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Check whether collapse ip -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} iq could be performed, ip boundary point; \textquotesingle{}mechanical\textquotesingle{} tests (positive jacobian) are not performed here ; iface = boundary face on which lie edge iedg -\/ in local face num. (pq, or ia in local tet notation). If isnm is 1, the collapse occurs along an external MG\+\_\+\+NOM edge. If isnmint is 1, ip is an internal non manifold point and dont have normals. In this last case, {\itshape lists}, {\itshape ilists} {\itshape refmin}, {\itshape refplus} and {\itshape isnm} variables aren\textquotesingle{}t used (we neither have a surfacic ball nor \char`\"{}positive\char`\"{} and \char`\"{}negative\char`\"{} volumes)

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
we don\textquotesingle{}t check edge lengths. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG5\_colver()}{MMG5\_colver()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily MMG5\+\_\+int MMG5\+\_\+colver (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{list,  }\item[{int}]{ilist,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{indq,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{typchk }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh \\
\hline
{\em met} & pointer to the metric \\
\hline
{\em list} & pointer to the ball of the point \\
\hline
{\em ilist} & number of elements in the ball of the point \\
\hline
{\em indq} & local index of the point on which we collapse \\
\hline
{\em typchk} & type of check performed depending on the remeshing step\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
np the index of the collpased point if success, 0 if we cannot collapse, -\/1 if we fail.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Collapse vertex p = list\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}\%4 of tetra list\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}/4 over vertex indq of tetra list\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}/4. Only physical tests (positive jacobian) are done (i.\+e. approximation of the surface, etc... must be performed outside). Merge tags and references of edges that will merge due to the collapse (the shell of each edge is travelled so each xtetra of the shell is updated). Note that it can\textquotesingle{}t be done in the previous loop because the mesh would be corrupted if we stop the collapse. It can\textquotesingle{}t neither be done in the next loop because we start to delete the elements of the shell.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG5\+\_\+coquilface (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{start,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{iface,  }\item[{int}]{ia,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{list,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{it1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{it2,  }\item[{int}]{silent }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\end{DoxyReturn}
Find all tets sharing edge {\itshape ia} of tetra {\itshape start}, and stores boundary faces when met. $ it1 $ and $ it2 = 6*iel + iface$, {\itshape iel} = index of tetra, {\itshape iface} = index of face in tetra.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Don\textquotesingle{}t work if {\itshape ia} has only one boundary face in its shell. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{libmmg3d__private_8h_a1dddec76046bc615430a4d7b882435e7}\label{libmmg3d__private_8h_a1dddec76046bc615430a4d7b882435e7}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG5\_intmet\_ani()}{MMG5\_intmet\_ani()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG5\+\_\+intmet\+\_\+ani (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{k,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{i,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ip,  }\item[{double}]{s }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em met} & pointer to the metric structure. \\
\hline
{\em k} & element index. \\
\hline
{\em i} & local index of edge in {\itshape k}. \\
\hline
{\em ip} & global index of the new point in which we want to compute the metric. \\
\hline
{\em s} & interpolation parameter (between 0 and 1). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if fail, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Interpolation of anisotropic sizemap at parameter {\itshape s} along edge {\itshape i} of elt {\itshape k} for a special storage of ridges metric (after defsiz call).

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
for boundary edges this function has to be called from a boundary face to ensure that the boundary edge will not be interpreted as an internal edge by error. It is due to the fact that regular boundary edges are not always marked as boundary inside a xtetra and tetra with boundary edges but no boundary faces are not always associated to an xtetra (moreover, for edges not belonging to a face inside the xtetra, the tag is not always up to date). 
\end{DoxyRemark}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG5\_mmg3dBezierCP()}{MMG5\_mmg3dBezierCP()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG5\+\_\+mmg3d\+Bezier\+CP (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structMMG5__Tria}{MMG5\+\_\+\+Tria}} $\ast$}]{pt,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{mmgcommon__private_8h_a76da89d731fcac55dc78dcd0e297da1e}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Bezier}}}]{pb,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{ori }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em pt} & pointer to the triangle structure. \\
\hline
{\em pb} & pointer to the computed Bezier structure. \\
\hline
{\em ori} & triangle orientation. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Compute Bezier control points on triangle {\itshape pt} (cf. \cite{vlachos2001curved})

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Todo}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{todo__todo000015}{Todo}}]merge with the MMG5\+\_\+mmgs\+Bezier\+CP function and remove the pointer toward this functions. \end{DoxyRefDesc}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item prior to commit f57b861966\+: we were comparing absolute values of normals projection (guessing that normals can be bad oriented). In this case, we can choose the wrong normal (normal at point related to other portion of surface) when the ridge angle is almost closed (smallest than 90°) because projection of normal at first triangle and normal at second triangle (or normal at point related to second surface) tends to -\/1;
\item the following assert on the positivity of at least one of the projections may fail but I think that it is not a normal behaviour\+: it means that the surface approximation has degenerated. See issue \#167
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyRemark}
Orientation of the normals at non-\/manifold points

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG5\_movbdyregpt\_ani()}{MMG5\_movbdyregpt\_ani()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG5\+\_\+movbdyregpt\+\_\+ani (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{PRoctree__3d__private_8h_a3123a024d89f849036a3b9c8397b5a9f}{MMG3\+D\+\_\+p\+PROctree}}}]{PROctree,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{listv,  }\item[{int}]{ilistv,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{lists,  }\item[{int}]{ilists,  }\item[{int}]{improve\+Surf,  }\item[{int}]{improve\+Vol }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em met} & pointer to the metric structure. \\
\hline
{\em PROctree} & pointer to the PROctree structure. \\
\hline
{\em listv} & pointer to the volumic ball of the point. \\
\hline
{\em ilistv} & size of the volumic ball. \\
\hline
{\em lists} & pointer to the surfacic ball of the point. \\
\hline
{\em ilists} & size of the surfacic ball. \\
\hline
{\em improve} & force the new minimum element quality to be greater or equal than 1.\+02 of the old minimum element quality.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if we can\textquotesingle{}t move the point, 1 if we can, -\/1 if we fail.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
we don\textquotesingle{}t check if we break the hausdorff criterion. 

the metric is not interpolated at the new position.
\end{DoxyRemark}
Move boundary regular point, whose volumic and surfacic balls are passed. Step 1 \+: rotation matrix that sends normal n to the third coordinate vector of R$^\wedge$3

Step 2 \+: rotation of the oriented surfacic ball with r \+: lispoi\mbox{[}k\mbox{]} is the common edge between faces lists\mbox{[}k-\/1\mbox{]} and lists\mbox{[}k\mbox{]}

Step 3 \+: Compute gradient towards optimal position = centre of mass of the ball, projected to tangent plane

Step 4 \+: locate new point in the ball, and compute its barycentric coordinates

Step 5 \+: come back to original problem, compute patch in triangle iel and check that geometric approx has not been degraded too much

Move boundary regular point, whose volumic and surfacic balls are passed.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
the metric is not interpolated at the new position. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
Step 1 \+: rotation matrix that sends normal n to the third coordinate vector of R$^\wedge$3

Step 2 \+: rotation of the oriented surfacic ball with r \+: lispoi\mbox{[}k\mbox{]} is the common edge between faces lists\mbox{[}k-\/1\mbox{]} and lists\mbox{[}k\mbox{]}

Step 3 \+: Compute optimal position to make current triangle equilateral, and average of these positions

Step 4 \+: locate new point in the ball, and compute its barycentric coordinates

Step 5 \+: come back to original problem, and compute patch in triangle iel

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG5\+\_\+movintpt\+LES\+\_\+iso (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{PRoctree__3d__private_8h_a3123a024d89f849036a3b9c8397b5a9f}{MMG3\+D\+\_\+p\+PROctree}}}]{PROctree,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{list,  }\item[{int}]{ilist,  }\item[{int}]{improve }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\

\hline

\hline
{\em improve} & force the new minimum element quality to be greater or equal than 0.\+9 of the old minimum element quality.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if we can\textquotesingle{}t move the point, 1 if we can.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Move internal point whose volumic ball is passed (for LES optimization). The optimal point position is computed as the barycenter of the optimal point position for each tetra. The optimal point position for a tetra is the point located over the normal of the face at the face barycenter and at the distance 1 of the face.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
the metric is not interpolated at the new position. 

we don\textquotesingle{}t check if we break the hausdorff criterion. 

not used. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{libmmg3d__private_8h_a71647aba5005f6b4a8b98d848493d565}\label{libmmg3d__private_8h_a71647aba5005f6b4a8b98d848493d565}} 
\index{libmmg3d\_private.h@{libmmg3d\_private.h}!MMG5\_norver@{MMG5\_norver}}
\index{MMG5\_norver@{MMG5\_norver}!libmmg3d\_private.h@{libmmg3d\_private.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG5\_norver()}{MMG5\_norver()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG5\+\_\+norver (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to mesh \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if successful, 0 if failed
\end{DoxyReturn}
Compute normals at C1 vertices, for C0\+: tangents.

Following list summerizes computed (and not computed) data depending on point type\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Corner point (MG\+\_\+\+CRN)\+: nothing (and no xpoint);
\item Reference point (MG\+\_\+\+REF)\+: xp, tangent (ppt-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}n), 1 normal (pxp-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}n1);
\item Ridge point (MG\+\_\+\+GEO)\+: xp, tangent,2 normals (pxp-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}n1 and n2);
\item Non-\/manifold point (MG\+\_\+\+NOM) are not filled here but in {\itshape nmgeom} function
\item Open boundary points (MG\+\_\+\+OPNBDY) are non-\/manifold so they are filled in nmgeom too.
\item Required points are analyzed using their other flags (so they may have an xpoint and a normal) but their normal is not used during remeshing.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Normals at regular boundary points can be provided by users but are ignored along featured edges. recomputation of normals only if mesh-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}xpoint has been freed

Step 1\+: identify boundary points

input normals are ignored along all type of featured edges (ref, geo, nom) but it is possible to implement their taking into account along non-\/ridges reference edges and external non-\/manifold ones.

Step 2\+: Allocate memory to store normals for boundary points

Step 3\+: compute normals + tangents

At C1 point

along ridge-\/curve

Along ridge\+: compute tangent as intersection of n1 + n2

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG5\_setadj()}{MMG5\_setadj()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG5\+\_\+setadj (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer towarad the mesh structure. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if fail, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
topology\+: set tria adjacency, detect Moebius, flip faces, count connected comp.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
\+: as all triangles are mesh boundaries, we do not need to mark their adges as MG\+\_\+\+BDY so the MG\+\_\+\+BDY tag may be used inside geometrical triangles (external non-\/parallel, or internal parallel) to tag edges on the intersection with purely parallel (non-\/geometrical) triangles. The MG\+\_\+\+PARBDYBDY tag is also added, as it does not have a supporting triangle to inherit this tag from.

REQ, NOSURF, etc... tags are added only inside xtetra. 

In openbdy mode, all non-\/manifold edges are marked as opnbdy. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG5\+\_\+setdhd (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

check for ridges\+: dihedral angle Step 1\+: check input ridges provided by the user to remove those ones between triangles belonging to the same plane. This step has to be done prior the next one because we want to remove the MG\+\_\+\+GEO tag transfered from ridges that we delete toward vertices by {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+setadj} but we want to preserve the MG\+\_\+\+GEO tags at vertices of ridges that will be added by the next step.

Step 2\+: check ref and angle with neighbour to update ref tags and ridge ones

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG5\_setVertexNmTag()}{MMG5\_setVertexNmTag()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG5\+\_\+set\+Vertex\+Nm\+Tag (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{uint16\+\_\+t }]{funcuint16\+\_\+t }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if success, 0 if fail. Seek the non-\/required non-\/manifold points and try to analyse whether they are corner or required.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
We don\textquotesingle{}t know how to travel through the shell of a non-\/manifold point by triangle adjacency. Thus the work done here can\textquotesingle{}t be performed in the \mbox{\hyperlink{analys__3d_8c_adf0a0532d8cbbe69168f12a7d0e9dd75}{MMG5\+\_\+singul}} function.

a temporary array {\itshape tmp} is used instead of the tmp field of the points to not break the Par\+Mmg distributed analysis in which this field is used to store the global numbering of nodes. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
Seek the non-\/required non-\/manifold points and try to analyse whether they are corner or required.

Step 1\+: count the number or feature edges passing through each points

Step 2\+: add suitable point tags depending on the counted feature edges

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG5\+\_\+split1b (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{list,  }\item[{int}]{ret,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ip,  }\item[{int}]{cas,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{met\+Rid\+Typ,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{chk\+Rid\+Tet }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\hline

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
-\/1 if we fail, 0 if we don\textquotesingle{}t split the edge, 1 if success.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Split edge $list[0]\%6$, whose shell list is passed, introducing point {\itshape ip} Beware \+: shell has to be enumerated in ONLY ONE TRAVEL (always same sense). 2 different checks \+: 1) are we creating a too small edge (BUG\+\_\+\+Split1b\+\_\+\+Spere\+Iso\+\_\+0.\+125h\+\_\+met) 2) in aniso and from the last wave of anatet(typchk=1)\+: avoid the creation of a tetra with 4 ridge vertices.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily const uint8\+\_\+t MMG5\+\_\+permedge\mbox{[}12\mbox{]}\mbox{[}6\mbox{]}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

{\bfseries Initial value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{=\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \{0,1,2,3,4,5\},\ \{1,2,0,5,3,4\},\ \{2,0,1,4,5,3\},\ \{0,4,3,2,1,5\},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \{3,0,4,1,5,2\},\ \{4,3,0,5,2,1\},\ \{1,3,5,0,2,4\},\ \{3,5,1,4,0,2\},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \{5,1,3,2,4,0\},\ \{2,5,4,1,0,3\},\ \{4,2,5,0,3,1\},\ \{5,4,2,3,1,0\}\ \}}

\end{DoxyCode}
Table that associates to each (even) permutation of the 4 vertices of a tetrahedron the corresponding permutation of its edges.~\newline
 Labels \+: 0 \+: \mbox{[}0,1,2,3\mbox{]} 1 \+: \mbox{[}0,2,3,1\mbox{]} 2 \+: \mbox{[}0,3,1,2\mbox{]} 3 \+: \mbox{[}1,0,3,2\mbox{]} 4 \+: \mbox{[}1,2,0,3\mbox{]} 5 \+: \mbox{[}1,3,2,0\mbox{]} 6 \+: \mbox{[}2,0,1,3\mbox{]} 7 \+: \mbox{[}2,1,3,0\mbox{]} 8 \+: \mbox{[}2,3,0,1\mbox{]} 9 \+: \mbox{[}3,0,2,1\mbox{]} 10 \+: \mbox{[}3,1,0,2\mbox{]} 11 \+: \mbox{[}3,2,1,0\mbox{]} The edge 0 of the config 1 become the edge 1 of the reference config so permedge\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}=1 ...
